Disinfect the Roller Head with Medical grade alcohol before and after each use. Cleans the skin in the treated area.<br />4.3. Roll over the skin while applying slight pressure in horizontal, vertical and diagonal directions on each part of the treated area. After rolling, my face is slightly pink for a couple of hours but I never draw blood.<br /><br />As compared to other rollers, the Derma-Logi roller has a much higher number of very fine needles and is a well-constructed tool with a curved handle that is easy to hold firmly.   230. One star, at best. This roller is wrong on many levels. The most critical flaws are:<br /><br />- the &#34;needles&#34; are NOT needles! They are BLADES! You end up with unevenly sliced skin in strip/line pattern, as opposed to the grid-like punctures you need.
